\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
4J-\/\+JEV:\+ Java version exposed the static instance of each stat.

This was inconvient for me as I needed to structure the stats/\+achievements differently on Durango.

Using getters like this means we can use different \doxylink{class_stats}{Stats} easilly on different platforms and still have a convenient identifier to use to award them. 

Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{_generic_stats_8h_source_l00020}{20}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{_generic_stats_8h_source}{Generic\+Stats.\+h}}.
